## Monograph

1. al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān  
   البرهان في وجوه البيان  
   Abū l-Ḥasan Isḥāq b. Ibrāhīm b. Sulaymān b. Wahab al-Kātib  
   (d. 4th century/10th century)

   **Editions**
    * *al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān* (n.plac., n.pub, 1930)
    * *al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān*, ed. ʿAbd al-Ḥamīd ʿIbādī (n.plac., n.pub, 1938)
    * *Kitāb Naqd al-nathr*, ed. ʿAbd al-Ḥamīd al-ʿAbbādī (Cairo: Lajnat al-Taʾlīf wa-l-Tarjama wa-l-Nashr, 1940)
    * *al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān*, ed. Aḥmad Maṭlūb (Baghdad: Jāmiʿat Baghdād, 1386/1967)
    * *al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān*, ed. Ḥifnī Muḥammad Sharaf (Cairo: Maktabat al-Shabāb, 1389/1969)
    * *Kitāb Naqd al-nathr* (Beirut: Dār al-Kutub al-ʿIlmiyya, 1980)
    * *Kitāb Naqd al-nathr* (Beirut: Dār al-Kutub al-ʿIlmiyya, 1982)
    * *Kitāb Naqd al-nathr* (Sousse: Dār al-Maʿārif lil-Ṭibāʿa wa-l-Nashr, 2004)
    * *al-Burhān fī wujūh al-bayān* (Riyadh: Maktabat al-Rushd Nāshirūn, 2012)

1. al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa  
   الذريعة إلى أصول الشريعة  
   ʿAlī b. al-Ḥusayn al-Sharīf al-Murtaḍā  
   (d. 436/1044)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * University of California, Los Angeles (#MS164), dated 5th-9th centuries/11th-15th centuries
    * Majlis, Tehran (#3185), dated 969/1561
    * Majlis, Tehran (#3794), dated 1025/1616
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#6519), dated 1027/1618
    * Maktabat Amīr al-Muʾminīn, Najaf (#140), dated 1042/1632-33

   **Editions**
    * *al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ed. Abū l-Qāsim al-Gurjī (Tehran: Intishārāt-i Dānishgāh-i Tehrān, 1346Sh/1967)
    * *al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ed. Abū l-Qāsim al-Gurjī (Tehran: Intishārāt-i Dānishgāh-i Tehrān, 1363Sh/1985)
    * *al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ed. Abū l-Qāsim al-Gurjī (Tehran: Intishārāt-i Dānishgāh-i Tehrān, 1376Sh/1998)
    * *al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ed. al-Lajna al-ʿIlmiyya fī Muʾassasat al-Imām al-Ṣādiq (Qum: Muʾassasat al-Imām al-Ṣādiq, 1387Sh/2008)
    * *al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ed. al-Sayyid ʿAlī Riḍā al-Madadī (Mashhad: Bunyād-i Pazhūhishhā-yi Islāmī – Āstān-i Quds-i Raḍawī, 1399Sh/2020)

   **Commentaries**
    * *Sharḥ al-Dharīʿa*, Kamāl al-Dīn al-Murtaḍā b. al-Muntahā b. al-Ḥusayn b. ʿAlī al-Ḥusaynī al-Marʿashī (d. after 525/1130)
    * *Sharḥ masāʾil al-Dharīʿa*, Muḥammad b. ʿAlī al-Ṭabarī (fl. 553/1158)
    * *al-Mustaqṣā fī sharḥ al-Dharīʿa*, Hibatallāh 'Quṭb al-Dīn al-Rāwandī (d. 573/1177)
    * *al-Iʿtibār ʿalā kitāb al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa*, ʿIzz al-Dīn Abū Ḥāmid ʿAbd al-Ḥamīd b. Hibatallāh b. Muḥammad (b. Muḥammad) b. al-Ḥusayn b. Abī l-Ḥadīd al-Madāʾinī al-Baghdādī (d. 655 or 656/1257 or 1258)

1. al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl  
   العدة في أصول الفقه/عدة الأصول  
   Muḥammad b. al-Ḥasan al-Ṭūsī  
   (d. 460/1067)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * AQR, Mashhad (#2916), dated 518/1125

    * AQR, Mashhad (#2914), dated 1044/1634
    * Majlis, Tehran (N/A), dated 1046/1637
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#14523), dated 1047/1637-38

   **Editions**

    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl* (Bombay: n.pub, 1318/1900-01)
    * *ʿUddat al-uṣūl wa-bi-dhaylihi al-Ḥāshiya al-Khalīliyya*, ed. Muḥammad Mahdī Ṭāhā Najaf (Qum: Muʾassasat Āl al-Bayt, 1403/1982)
    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Riḍā al-Anṣārī al-Qummī (Qum: n.p., 1376Sh/1997)
    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Mahdī Ṭāhā Najaf (Qum: Sitāra, 1375Sh/1997)
    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Riḍā al-Anṣārī al-Qummī (Qum: Muḥammad Taqī ʿAlāqbandiyān, 1375Sh/1997)
    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl* (Qum: Muʾassasat al-Biʿtha, 1417/1997)
    * *al-ʿUdda fī uṣūl al-fiqh/ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Riḍā al-Anṣārī al-Qummī (Qum: Bustān-i Kitāb, 1389Sh/2010)
    * *ʿUddat al-uṣūl* (Tehran: Maṭbaʿ Mīrzā Ḥabīballāh, 1278Sh/1899-1900)

   **Commentaries**
    * *Ḥāshiyat ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, Khalīl b. al-Ghāzī al-Qazwīnī (d. 1089/1678)
    * *Najāt al-muslimīn wa-munjī l-hālikīn*, Muḥammad Mahdī b. Muḥammad Bāqir al-Ḥusaynī al-Mashhadī (d. 11th century/17th century)
    * *Tanqīḥ al-marām fī Ḥāshiyat Sharḥ ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ʿAlī Aṣghar b. Muḥammad Yūsuf al-Qazwīnī (d. 1120/1709)
    * *Ḥāshiyat Sharḥ ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, ʿAlī Aṣghar b. Muḥammad Yūsuf al-Qazwīnī (d. 1120/1709)
    * *Sharḥ ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, Muḥammad b. Muḥammad Ṣādiq al-Ḥusaynī al-Qazwīnī (d. 12th century/18th century)
    * *Ḥāshiyat Ḥāshiyat ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, Muḥammad Bāqir b. Ghāzī al-Qazwīnī (d. 12th century/18th century)
    * *Tuḥaf al-ʿuqūl fī sharḥ ʿUddat al-uṣūl*, Khiḍr b. Ismāʿīl al-Ashrafī al-Māzandarānī (d. *c.* 1336/1917)

1. Ghunyat al-nuzūʿ ilā ʿilmay al-uṣūl wa-l-furūʿ  
   غنية النزوع إلى علمي الأصول والفروع  
   Ḥamza b. ʿAlī  
   (d. 585/1189)

   **Editions**

    * *Ghunyat al-nuzūʿ ilā ʿilmay al-uṣūl wa-l-furūʿ* (Tehran: Majlis-i Shūrā-yi Islāmī, 1390/2011-12)

   **Commentaries**
    * *Muʿtaqad al-imāmiyya*, unknown (d. 999/1599)

1. Maʿārij al-uṣūl  
   معارج الأصول  
   Jaʿfar b. al-Ḥasan al-Muḥaqqiq al-Ḥillī  
   (d. 676/1277)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Malek, Tehran (#1632/3), dated 707/1307
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#12640), dated 968/1561
    * AQR, Mashhad (#2968), dated 11th century/17th century
    * AQR, Mashhad (#13171/6), dated 11th century/17th century
    * Masjid-i Aʿẓam, Qum (#768/5), dated 11th century/17th century

   **Editions**
    * *Maʿārij al-uṣūl* (Tehran: n.pub, 1310/1892)
    * *Maʿārij al-uṣūl* (Tehran: n.pub, 1310/1893)
    * *Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Ḥusayn al-Raḍawī al-Kashmīrī (Qum: Muʾassasat Āl al-Bayt, 1403/1982)
    * *Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, ed. Muḥammad Ḥusayn al-Raḍawī al-Kashmīrī (London: Muʾassasat al-Imām ʿAlī, 2003)

   **Commentaries**
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Baʿḍ al-Aṣḥāb al-Mutaʾakhkhirīn ʿan al-Shahīd al-Thānī (d. after 966/1558)
    * *Ḥāshiya ʿalā Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Mullā Muḥammad Amīn al-Astarābādī (d. 1033 or 1036/1623 or 1626)
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Mīr ʿAbd al-Ṣamad al-Ḥusaynī al-Hamadānī (d. 1216/1802)
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Muḥammad b. ʿAlī al-Ṭabāṭabāʾī (d. 1242/1827)
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Ākhund Muḥammad Kāẓim b. Muḥammad ʿAlī al-Bihbahānī (d. 1250 or 1255/1834 or 1839)
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Mīrzā Bābā al-Sabzawārī (d. before 1293/1876)
    * *Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, Muḥammad Riḍā b. Muḥammad ʿAlī al-Isfirinjānī (d. 13th century/18th-19th century)
    * *Ḥāshiya ʿalā Maʿārij al-uṣūl*, ʿAbd al-Ḥusayn b. Jawād al-Baghdādī (d. 1365/1946)

   (d. 676/1277)

## Commentary (sharḥ)

1. Sharḥ al-Dharīʿa  
   شرح الذريعة  
   Kamāl al-Dīn al-Murtaḍā b. al-Muntahā b. al-Ḥusayn b. ʿAlī al-Ḥusaynī al-Marʿashī  
   (d. after 525/1130)

1. Sharḥ masāʾil al-Dharīʿa  
   شرح مسائل الذريعة  
   Muḥammad b. ʿAlī al-Ṭabarī  
   (fl. 553/1158)

1. al-Mustaqṣā fī sharḥ al-Dharīʿa  
   المستقصى في شرح الذريعة  
   Hibatallāh 'Quṭb al-Dīn al-Rāwandī  
   (d. 573/1177)

1. al-Iʿtibār ʿalā kitāb al-Dharīʿa ilā uṣūl al-sharīʿa  
   الاعتبار على كتاب الذريعة إلى أصول الشريعة  
   ʿIzz al-Dīn Abū Ḥāmid ʿAbd al-Ḥamīd b. Hibatallāh b. Muḥammad (b. Muḥammad) b. al-Ḥusayn b. Abī l-Ḥadīd al-Madāʾinī al-Baghdādī  
   (d. 655 or 656/1257 or 1258)

1. Ghāyat al-bādiʾ fī sharḥ al-Mabādiʾ  
   غاية البادئ في شرح المبادئ  
   Muḥammad ibn ʿAlī ibn Muḥammad al-Jurjānī al-Gharawī  
   (fl. 698/1298)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Majlis, Tehran (#7064), dated 717/1318
    * AQR, Mashhad (#2921), dated 8th century/14th century
    * University of Isfahan, Isfahan (#380), dated 884/1479
    * AQR, Mashhad (#19751), dated 9th century/15th century
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#6672), dated 10th century/16th century

   **Editions**
    * *Ghāyat al-bādiʾ fī sharḥ al-Mabādiʾ* (Tehran: Kitābkhāna-yi Majlis-i Shūrā-yi Islāmī, 1397Sh/2018-19)

1. al-Wāfī fī sharḥ Mukhtaṣar al-uṣūl  
   الوافي في شرح مختصر الأصول  
   unknown  
   (d. 8th century/13th century)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Malek, Tehran (#1155), dated 743/1343

1. Sharḥ Mukhtaṣar al-uṣūl

   al-Ḥasan ibn Yūsuf al-Ḥillī  
   (d. 726/1325)

    * KG, Najaf (#436)

   غاية الوصول وإيضاح السبل في شرح مختصر منتهى السؤل والأمل في علمي الأصول والجدل  
   al-Ḥasan ibn Yūsuf al-Ḥillī

   **Commentaries**

## Gloss (ḥāshīya)

1. Ḥāshiyat Tahdhīb al-wuṣūl ilā ʿilm al-uṣūl  
   حاشية تهذيب الوصول إلى علم الأصول  
   unknown  
   (d. 8th century/14th century)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#12843), dated 8th century/14th century

   (d. *c.* 877/1472)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * AQR, Mashhad (#2968), dated 882/1477

   ʿAlī b. Muḥammad al-Ṭūsī  
   (d. *c.* 877/1472)

   **Principle Manuscripts**

## Marginal notes (taʿlīqa)

1. Taʿlīqāt ʿalā Ḥāshiyat Sharḥ al-Mukhtaṣar  
   تعليقات على حاشية شرح المختصر

    * Majlis, Tehran (#18391)

   al-Mīrzā ʿAlāʾ al-Dīn Ḥusayn b. Rafīʿ al-Dīn Muḥammad al-Marʿashī al-Āmūlī  
   (d. 1064/1653)

## Summary (khulāṣa/mukhtaṣar)

1. Mukhtaṣar al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh  
   مختصر التذكرة بأصول الفقه  
   Abū l-Fatḥ Muḥammad b. ʿAlī b.ʿUthmān al-Ṭarāblusī al-Karājukī  
   (d. 449/1057)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Markaz-i Muṭālaʿāt, Qum (#499/3)

   **Editions**
    * *Mukhtaṣar al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh* (Tabriz: n.pub, 1322/1904)
    * *Mukhtaṣar al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh*, ed. Mahdī Najaf (Qum: Kungara-yi Shaykh Mufīd, 1413/1992)
    * *Mukhtaṣar al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh*, ed. Mahdī Najaf (Beirut: Dār al-Mufīd li-Ṭibāʿa wa-l-Nashr wa-l-Tawzīʿ, 1414/1993)

1. Naḍd al-qawāʿid al-fiqhiyya ʿalā madhhab al-imāmiyya  
   نضد القواعد الفقهية على مذهب الإمامية  
   Miqdād b. ʿAbdallāh b. Muḥammad b. al-Ḥusayn b. Muḥammad  
   (d. 826/1422)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Malek, Tehran (#1954/2), dated 11th century/17th century
    * AQR, Mashhad (#21566), dated 11th century/17th century
    * AQR, Mashhad (#2663), dated 11th century/17th century
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#11647/5), dated 11th century/17th century
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#2508), dated 1288/1871

   **Editions**
    * *Naḍd al-qawāʿid al-fiqhiyya ʿalā madhhab al-imāmiyya* (Qum: Manshūrāt Maktabat Āyatullāh al-ʿUẓmā al-Marʿashī al-Najafī, 1361Sh/1981)

1. Uṣūl al-fiqh/al-Adilla ʿalā mashrūʿiyyat al-ʿamal bi-l-ẓunūn  
   أصول الفقه/الأدلة على مشروعية العمل بالظنون  
   Fakhr al-Dīn b. Muḥammad ʿAlī b. Aḥmad al-Ṭurayḥī al-Najafī  
   (d. 1085 or 1087/1674 or 1676)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Adabiyyāt, Tehran (#383/1), dated 11th century/17th century
    * AQR, Mashhad (#15245/3), dated 1258/1842
    * Gulpāygānī, Qum (#60/52-9112/2)
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#3028/3)

## Poem (manẓūma)

1. Naẓm al-uṣūl  
   نظم الأصول  
   Muḥammad b. al-Ḥusayn Bahāʾ al-Dīn al-ʿĀmilī  
   (d. 1030 or 1031/1620 or 1621)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * AQR, Mashhad (#27588), dated 1226/1811

1. Irshād al-ṭālib ilā manẓūmat al-kawākib  
   إرشاد الطالب إلى منظومة الكواكب  
   Muḥammad b. Ḥasan al-Kawākibī  
   (d. 1096/1684-85)

   (alive in 1104/1693)

## Refutation (radd)

1. Nuṣrat al-aṣḥāb  
   نصرة الأصحاب  
   ʿAlī Naqī b. Muḥammad Hāshim al-Ṭughāʾī al-Kamaraʾī  
   (d. *c.* 1060/1650)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * ʿAllāma Ṭabātabaʾī, Shiraz (#17)

1. Shubhat al-dawr/al-Radd ʿalā Mullā Khalīl al-Qazwīnī  
   شبهة الدور/الرد على ملا خليل القزويني  
   al-Ḥusayn b. Jamāl al-Dīn Muḥammad Āqā Ḥusayn al-Khwānsārī  
   (d. 1099/1687-8)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Madrasa-yi Miʿmārbāshī, Tehran (#99/7), dated 1089/1678
    * Majlis, Tehran (#18386/8), dated 1090/1679
    * Sipahsālār, Tehran (#1374/8), dated 1093/1682
    * Marwī, Tehran (#800/10), dated 1098/1686
    * Marʿashī, Qum (#5403/2), dated 11th century/17th century

   **Commentaries**
    * *Radd Shubhat al-dawr*, Muḥammad Ḥusayn b. Muḥammad Bāqir al-Yazdī (d. 11th century/17th century)

1. Radd Shubhat al-dawr

   (d. 11th century/17th century)

1. Bughyat al-ṭālibīn li-ṣiḥḥat ṭarīqat al-mujtahidīn

## Translation

1. Ijtihād wa taqlīd  
   اجتهاد و تقليد  
   Maḥmūd al-Ḥusaynī al-Ṭabāṭabāʾī  
   (d. 11th century/17th century)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Gulpāygānī, Qum (#36/166-6796/3)

1. Maʿālim al-uṣūl  
   معالم الأصول  
   Muḥammad Hādī b. Muḥammad Ṣāliḥ al-Māzandarānī  
   (d. 1120/1708-9)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * Gulpāygānī, Qum (#6/73-983), dated 11th century/17th century
    * Markaz-i Iḥyāʾ, Qum (#3935), dated 1149/1736
    * Saryazdī, Yazd (#173/2), dated 13th century/19th century

   **Editions**
    * *Maʿālim al-uṣul*, ed. Murtaḍā Mudarissī Chāhārdahī (Tehran: Kitābfurūshī-yi Shafīʿī; Muʾssasat ʿAbd al-Raḥīm ʿIlmī, 1379/1959)

1. Asās al-uṣūl  
   أساس الأصول  
   Ḥimāyat Ḥusayn al-Nīshābūrī al-Kantūrī  
   (d. 13th century/19th century)

   **Principle Manuscripts**
    * AQR, Mashhad (#22134), dated 13th century/19th century
    * AQR, Mashhad (#19045), dated 13th century/19th century

1. Fiqh-i istidlālī/Tarjuma-yi bakhsh-i Ghunyat al-nuzūʿ ilā ʿilmay al-uṣūl wa-l-furūʿ  
   فقه استدلالی/ترجمه بخش فقه غنیة النزوع إلی علمی الأصول والفروع  
   Mahdī Anjawinizhād  
   

   **Editions**
    * *Fiqh-i istidlālī/Tarjuma-yi bakhsh-i Ghunyat al-nuzūʿ ilā ʿilmay al-uṣūl wa-l-furūʿ*, ed. Mahdī Anjawīnizhād (Mashhad: Dānishgāh-i Firdawsī-yi Mashhad, 1374Sh/1995-6)

1. Safīnat al-najāt  
   سفينة النجاة  
   Muḥammad Riḍā al-Tafrīshī al-Nāqūsānī  
   (d. 1364/1944)

   **Editions**
    * *Safīnat al-najāt*, ed. Muḥammad Riḍā al-Tafrishī al-Naqūsānī (n.plac., n.p, 1379/1959)

1. Anwār al-uṣūl fī Maʿālim al-uṣūl  
   أنوار الأصول في معالم الأصول  
   Bilāl Ḥusayn Jaʿfarī  
   

   **Editions**
    * *Anwār al-uṣūl fī Maʿālim al-uṣūl* (Qum: al-Ṭayyār, 1383Sh/2004)

## Unknown

1. al-Mutamassik bi-ḥabl āl al-rasūl  
   المتمسك بحبل آل الرسول  
   al-Ḥasan b. ʿAlī Ibn Abī ʿAqīl al-ʿUmmānī  
   (d. 3rd century/6th century)

1. al-Alfāẓ  
   الألفاظ  
   Hishām b. al-Ḥakam  
   (d. 179/795)

1. Ikhtilāf al-ḥadīth  
   اختلاف الحديث  
   Yūnus b. ʿAbd al-Raḥmān  
   (d. 208/823-4)

1. Ikhtilaf al-ḥadīth  
   اختلاف الحديث  
   Muḥammad b. Abī ʿUmayr Ziyād b. ʿĪsā, Abū Aḥmad al-Azdī  
   (d. 217/832)

1. Kitāb al-khuṣūṣ wa-l-ʿumūm  
   كتاب الخصوص والعموم  
   Ismāʿīl b. ʿAlī b. Isḥāq Abū Sahl al-Nawbakhtī  
   (alive in 232/846)

1. Kitāb naqḍ ijtihād al-raʾy ʿalā Ibn al-Rāwandī  
   كتاب نقد اجتهاد الرأي على ابن الراوندي  
   Ismāʿīl b. ʿAlī b. Isḥāq Abū Sahl al-Nawbakhtī  
   (alive in 232/846)

1. Kitāb al-asmāʾ wa-l-aḥkām  
   كتاب الأسماء والأحكام  
   Ismāʿīl b. ʿAlī b. Isḥāq Abū Sahl al-Nawbakhtī  
   (alive in 232/846)

1. Kitāb ibṭāl al-qiyās  
   كتاب إبطال القياس  
   Ismāʿīl b. ʿAlī b. Isḥāq Abū Sahl al-Nawbakhtī  
   (alive in 232/846)

1. al-Qiyās  
   القياس  
   ʿAbdallāh b. Jaʿfar al-Ḥimyarī  
   (d. 293 or 305/905 or 917)

1. Kitāb masāʾil al-ḥadīthayn al-mukhtalifayn  
   كتاب مسائل الحديثين المختلفين  
   Muḥammad b. Aḥmad Ibn Dāwūd  
   (d. 368/978)

1. Kitāb masʾala fī l-qiyās mukhtaṣar  
   كتاب مسئلة في القياس مختصر  
   Muḥammad b. Muḥammad b. al-Nuʿmān al-ʿUkbarī al-Baghdādī  
   (d. 413/1022)

1. al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh  
   التذكرة بأصول الفقه  
   Muḥammad b. Muḥammad b. al-Nuʿmān al-ʿUkbarī al-Baghdādī  
   (d. 413/1022)

   **Commentaries**
    * *Mukhtaṣar al-Tadhkira bi-uṣūl al-fiqh*, Abū l-Fatḥ Muḥammad b. ʿAlī b.ʿUthmān al-Ṭarāblusī al-Karājukī (d. 449/1057)

1. Kitāb fī l-qiyās  
   كتاب في القياس  
   Muḥammad b. Muḥammad b. al-Nuʿmān al-ʿUkbarī al-Baghdādī  
   (d. 413/1022)

1. al-Masāʾil al-Mūsiliyāt -thalāth fī l-waʿīd wa-l-qiyās wa-l-iʿtimād  
   المسائل الموصليات - ثلاث في الوعيد والقياس والاعتماد  
   ʿAlī b. al-Ḥusayn al-Sharīf al-Murtaḍā  
   (d. 436/1044)

1. Kitāb al-khilāf fī uṣūl al-fiqh  
   كتاب الخلاف في أصول الفقه  
   ʿAlī b. al-Ḥusayn al-Sharīf al-Murtaḍā  
   (d. 436/1044)

1. al-Taʿlīq ʿalā Kitāb al-ʿumad li-l-Qāḍī ʿAbd al-Jabbār  
   التعليق على كتاب العمد للقاضي عبد الجبار  
   ʿAlī b. al-Ḥusayn al-Sharīf al-Murtaḍā  
   (d. 436/1044)

1. al-Taqrīb fī uṣūl al-fiqh  
   التقريب في أصول الفقه  
   Abū Yaʿlā Ḥamza b. ʿAbd al-ʿAzīz al-Daylamī, Sallār al-Daylamī  
   (d. 448 or 463/1056 or 1071)

1. Masʾala fī l-ʿamal bi-khabar al-wāḥid wa-bayān ḥujjiyyatih  
   مسألة في العمل بخبر الواحد وبيان حجيته  
   Muḥammad b. al-Ḥasan al-Ṭūsī  
   (d. 460/1067)

1. al-Naqḍ ʿalā Ibn Shādhān fī masʿalat al-ghār  
   النقض على ابن شاذان في مسئلة الغار  
   Muḥammad b. al-Ḥasan al-Ṭūsī  
   (d. 460/1067)

1. Kitāb fī ibṭāl al-qiyās  
   كتاب في إبطال القياس  
   Yaḥyā Abū Muḥammad al-ʿAlawī  
   (d. 4th or 5th century/10th or 11th century)

1. Talkhīṣ masāʾil al-Dharīʿa  
   تلخيص مسائل الذريعة  
   Abū l-Ḥasan ʿAlī b. Zayd b. Muḥammad Farīd Kharasān al-Bayhaqī/al-Bīhaqī  
   (d. 565/1170)

1. Sharḥ wa-taʿlīq ʿalā al-Dharīʿa  
   شرح وتعليق على الذريعة  
   Murtaḍā b. Muntahā al-Ḥusaynī al-Marʿashī  
   (d. 6th century/12th century)

1. al-Maṣādir fī uṣūl al-fiqh  
   المصادر في أصول الفقه  
   Sadīd al-Dīn Maḥmūd b. ʿAlī al-Ḥimmaṣī al-Rāzī  
   (d. *c.* 600/1203)

1. al-Munqidh min al-taqlīd wa-l-murshid ilā l-tawḥīd  
   المنقذ من التقليد والمرشد إلى التوحيد  
   Sadīd al-Dīn Maḥmūd b. ʿAlī al-Ḥimmaṣī al-Rāzī  
   (d. *c.* 600/1203)

1. al-Tabyīn wa-l-tanqīḥ fī l-taḥsīn wa-l-taqbīḥ  
   التبيين والتنقيح في التحسين والتقبيح  
   Sadīd al-Dīn Maḥmūd b. ʿAlī al-Ḥimmaṣī al-Rāzī  
   (d. *c.* 600/1203)

1. al-Nukat al-badīʿa fī taḥrīr al-Dharīʿa  
   النكت البديعة في تحرير الذريعة  
   al-Ḥasan ibn Yūsuf al-Ḥillī  
   (d. 726/1325)

1. Sharḥ Ghāyat al-wuṣūl ilā ʿilm al-uṣūl  
   شرح غاية الوصول إلى علم الأصول  
   al-Ḥasan ibn Yūsuf al-Ḥillī  
   (d. 726/1325)

1. Sharḥ Maʿārij al-uṣūl  
   شرح معارج الأصول  
   Mīr Fayḍullāh ibn ʿAbd al-Qāhir al-Ḥusaynī al-Najafī al-Tafrīshī  
   (d. 1125/1616)

1. Niẓām al-fuṣūl fī sharḥ Nahj al-wuṣūl ilā maʿrifat al-uṣūl  
   نظام الفصول في شرح نهج الوصول إلى معرفة الأصول  
   Fatḥallāh b. ʿUlwān al-Dawraqī  
   (d. 1130/1718)

1. Uṣūl Āl al-Rasūl  
   أصول آل الرسول  
   Muḥammad Hāshim b. Zayn al-ʿĀbidīn al-Mūsawī al-Khurāsānī al-Iṣfahānī al-Chahārsūqī  
   (d. 17 Ramaḍān 1318/8 January 1901)

1. Kitāb Kashf al-tamwīh wa-l-iltibās fī ibṭāl al-qiyās

   Muḥammad b. Aḥmad Ibn Junayd al-Iskāfī  
   (d. between 366-377/977-988)

   Abū Muḥammad Yaḥyā b. Aḥmad al-ʿAlawī al-Nayshābūrī  
   (d. *c.* 350/961)

1. Ibṭāl al-qiyās  
   إبطال القياس  
   Abū Muḥammad Yaḥyā b. Aḥmad al-ʿAlawī al-Nayshābūrī  
   (d. *c.* 350/961)

1. Kitāb al-istifāda fī l-ṭuʿūn ʿalā l-awāʾil wa-l-radd ʿalā aṣḥāb al-ijtihād wa-l-qiyās  
   كتاب الاستفادة في الطعون على الأوائل والرد على أصحاب الاجتهاد والقياس  
   ʿAbdallāh b. ʿAbd al-Raḥmān al-Zubayrī  
   (d. 4th or 5th century/10th or 11th century)

1. Kitāb al-radd ʿalā ahl al-qiyās  
   كتاب الرد على أهل القياس  
   ʿAlī b. ʿAbdallāh b. ʿImrān al-Qurashī Abū l-Ḥasan al-Makhzūmī al-Maymūnī  
   (d. 5th century/11th century)
